"""Font-profile → synthesis spacing fallback wiring (M3).

These tests prove that the merchant font profile (PR #994) is used ONLY as a
fallback for scaffolds that cannot measure their own item-region geometry, and
never overrides real measured geometry — so the structure gate is unaffected for
receipts that can measure themselves.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from receipt_agent.agents.label_evaluator.merchant_synthesis import (
    MerchantAnalysis,
    MerchantLineItem,
    _font_geometry_px,
    _line_step,
    _template_fill_geometry,
)

FONT_GEOMETRY = {
    "char_width_px": 23.0,
    "font_height_px": 20.0,
    "line_step_px": 31.0,
    "price_column_x_px": 880.0,
    "char_aspect": 1.7,
}


def _bare_analysis(receipt):
    return MerchantAnalysis(
        receipt=receipt,
        line_items=[],
        subtotal=None,
        tax_total=None,
        grand_total=None,
        grand_total_line_indices=[],
    )


def test_template_geometry_uses_profile_fallback_when_unmeasurable():
    # No item-region words to measure (no line_items -> empty band), so the
    # char width / height / price column fall back to the merchant profile.
    receipt = {"lines": [], "font_geometry": FONT_GEOMETRY}
    geo = _template_fill_geometry(_bare_analysis(receipt))
    assert geo["char_w"] == 23
    assert geo["height"] == 20
    # price center (880) + half price width (3*char_w) capped at 996.
    assert geo["price_x1"] == min(880 + 3 * 23, 996)


def test_template_geometry_uses_constants_without_profile():
    receipt = {"lines": []}
    geo = _template_fill_geometry(_bare_analysis(receipt))
    assert geo["char_w"] == 16
    assert geo["height"] == 18


def test_template_geometry_prefers_measured_over_profile():
    # A measurable item band must win over the profile fallback.
    receipt = {
        "lines": [
            {
                "line_id": 0,
                "words": [
                    {"text": "BANANAS", "bbox": [80, 500, 220, 520],
                     "labels": ["PRODUCT_NAME"]},
                    {"text": "1.99", "bbox": [860, 500, 900, 520],
                     "labels": ["LINE_TOTAL"]},
                ],
            }
        ],
        "font_geometry": FONT_GEOMETRY,
    }
    item = MerchantLineItem(
        line_index=0,
        line_indices=[0],
        amount=__import__("decimal").Decimal("1.99"),
        product_text="BANANAS",
        center_y=510,
        taxable=False,
        band_line_indices=[0],
    )
    analysis = MerchantAnalysis(
        receipt=receipt,
        line_items=[item],
        subtotal=None,
        tax_total=None,
        grand_total=None,
        grand_total_line_indices=[],
    )
    geo = _template_fill_geometry(analysis)
    # measured char width = median(140/7, 40/4) = median(20, 10) = 15, which is
    # the receipt's own measurement, NOT the profile's 23.
    assert geo["char_w"] == 15
    # price column anchored on the real LINE_TOTAL center (880) + 3*char_w(15).
    assert geo["price_x1"] == 880 + 3 * 15


def test_line_step_uses_profile_fallback_only_when_opted_in():
    # Generation/layout call sites opt in -> profile pitch is used.
    receipt = {"lines": [], "font_geometry": FONT_GEOMETRY}
    assert _line_step([], receipt, allow_font_geometry_fallback=True) == 31


def test_line_step_scoring_path_ignores_profile():
    from receipt_agent.agents.label_evaluator.merchant_synthesis import (
        _DEFAULT_LINE_STEP,
    )

    # Default (scoring/signature) path must NOT use the profile, so the
    # structure-similarity gate and emitted evidence stay measurement-only.
    receipt = {"lines": [], "font_geometry": FONT_GEOMETRY}
    assert _line_step([], receipt) == _DEFAULT_LINE_STEP


def test_line_step_constant_without_profile():
    from receipt_agent.agents.label_evaluator.merchant_synthesis import (
        _DEFAULT_LINE_STEP,
    )

    assert (
        _line_step([], {"lines": []}, allow_font_geometry_fallback=True)
        == _DEFAULT_LINE_STEP
    )


def test_font_geometry_px_rejects_missing_and_nonpositive():
    assert _font_geometry_px({}, "char_width_px", default=16) == 16
    assert _font_geometry_px({"x": None}, "x", default=16) == 16
    assert _font_geometry_px({"x": 0}, "x", default=16) == 16
    assert _font_geometry_px({"x": -5}, "x", default=16) == 16
    assert _font_geometry_px({"x": 22.6}, "x", default=16) == 23

codex
Plan: kill per-token rendering first; grid typography is the blocker, and texture/graphics only matter after that.

**1. Typography**
D1 Font: adopt VileR Ultimate Oldschool PC Font Pack `Bm437 IBM VGA 8x16` as the bundled default. It matches Epson Font A’s 8x16/0.5-ish grid better than VT323, avoids GPL font redistribution risk from `thermal-sans-mono`, and is acceptable for demo/training with attribution.

D2 Code: add `rendering/receipt_grid.py` with `build_grid_spec`, `group_words_into_grid_lines`, `draw_grid_line`, `draw_token_chars`. Change [receipt_renderer.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/rendering/receipt_renderer.py:77) `render_receipt` to group by line, pick one font size per line, set `draw.fontmode = "1"`, and place each glyph at `grid_left + col * cell_w` with `anchor="ls"`. Keep `_fit_font`/`_fit_condense` only for an explicit legacy fallback. Change `_draw_text` into the grid glyph drawer. Change `_load_font` to prefer the vendored Bm437 font. Extend [font_profile.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/rendering/font_profile.py:119) `MerchantFontProfile.to_geometry_params` with `cell_w_px`, `cell_h_px`, `estimated_columns`. Change [render_synthetic_receipts.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/scripts/render_synthetic_receipts.py:548) `_render_cached_hybrid` to enable grid mode and stop using `min_font_px/max_font_px` as the realism control.

D3 Dependencies: no pip dependency beyond Pillow. Add vendored TTF plus `NOTICE`/attribution. Offline risk is font availability; fail closed to existing system monospace only for tests.

D4 Order: first. Nothing else should be judged before this lands.

**2. Layout**
D1 Library: adopt `python-escpos` `software_columns` algorithm, but vendor our own 40-line MIT-attributed implementation. Do not add `python-escpos` or ReceiptLine at runtime.

D2 Code: extend `rendering/receipt_grid.py` with `GridCell`, `GridLine`, `layout_cells`, `wrap_cell`, `token_spans_to_bboxes`. Change [merchant_synthesis.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/merchant_synthesis.py:6453) `_line_step` and `_label_x_p50` to prefer grid metadata when present. Change `_template_fill_geometry`, `_build_template_filled_row`, `_build_line_item_line`, `_build_line`, `_right_align_money_box` to emit desc/price/tax-flag cells instead of freehand token rectangles. Change `render_receipt` to render a full grid line when `line["grid"]` exists, else infer grid from word boxes.

D3 Dependencies: stdlib `textwrap` only. Risk: wrapped item rows differ by merchant; make wrap policy per merchant profile.

D4 Order: second, immediately after typography. Can parallelize tests/metrics with content work once the grid API is stable.

**3. Content**
D1 Library: adopt `phonenumbers` only. Do not add Faker, faker-commerce, uszipcode, or usaddress for the demo path; use real corpus text plus static merchant profiles.

D2 Code: add `synthesis_content_profile.py` and `synthesis_receipt_model.py` for merchant grammar, tax letters, item-count semantics, and totals validation. Change `generate_merchant_synthesis_candidates` to attach a content profile and reject invalid candidates before return. Change `_compose_online_catalog_receipt`, `_write_composed_totals`, `_apply_non_taxable_delta`, `_apply_taxable_delta`, `_reconcile_item_count` to use one pure reconciliation function with hard assertions. Keep `synthesis_text_clean.clean_token_text` as a cleanup pass, not a generator.

D3 Dependencies: `phonenumbers`. Runtime risk is tiny. Static ZIP/address tables are safer than fake-data libraries for this use case.

D4 Order: third. Can run in parallel with graphics after item #2 defines row/cell grammar.

**4. Graphics**
D1 Library: adopt `treepoem` as the one graphics generator. It handles Code128, UPC-A, I2of5, and QR through BWIPP; standards-correct HRI beats the current fake random bars.

D2 Code: add `rendering/receipt_graphics.py` with `render_barcode_tile`, `render_qr_tile`, `graphics_profile_for_merchant`. Replace [render_synthetic_receipts.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/scripts/render_synthetic_receipts.py:674) `_draw_qr` and `_draw_barcode`; change `_overlay_qr_and_barcode` to paste generated tiles into real blank bands; keep `_overlay_cached_logo` but route logos through the same final degradation pass. Add merchant placement hints from `merchant_synthesis` metadata where available.

D3 Dependencies: `treepoem` pip plus system Ghostscript. Offline/CI risk is `gs` missing; detect once at startup and skip graphics with an explicit warning rather than silently drawing fake bars.

D4 Order: fourth. Can prototype independently on cached renders after typography lands.

**5. Paper Texture**
D1 Library: adopt Augraphy, but only after grid text and graphics are clean.

D2 Code: add `rendering/thermal_degradation.py` with `build_thermal_pipeline` and `apply_thermal_degradation`. Replace [render_synthetic_receipts.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/scripts/render_synthetic_receipts.py:514) `_composite_paper_texture` with a wrapper that does ink bleed, low ink lines, warm paper fog, subtle noise, small perspective, then JPEG last. Change `_render_cached_hybrid` to pass seed/profile. Do not apply geometric warps to ML-training images until bbox transforms are implemented.

D3 Dependencies: `augraphy`, `opencv-python`, `numpy`. Risk: heavy CPU and bbox desync. Keep it offline batch-only, seeded, and low-strength.

D4 Order: last. It can be visually tuned in parallel on exported PNGs, but merge after #1-#4.

**First-PR Scope**
Minimal PR: typography grid only. In `render_receipt`, replace per-token `_fit_font` with line grouping, derive `cell_w = profile.char_width * inner_w`, `cell_h = profile.line_pitch * inner_h` or `profile.font_height * inner_h * 1.35`, and `font_px = profile.font_height * inner_h` clamped to sane bounds. For each word, compute `start_col = round((word_left - grid_left) / cell_w)`, then draw each char at `start_col + i`.

Render text on a 1-bit/`L` mask with `fontmode="1"`, baseline `line_top + ascent`, `anchor="ls"`, then integer `NEAREST` upscale if using a lower native mask. Apply only the existing light texture after the crisp render. No layout grammar, no new content, no barcodes.

A/B: render the same cached matrix with legacy vs grid using identical seeds. Measure `font_height_cv_by_line`, `price_decimal_x_stddev`, OCR/re-OCR pass rate, and line-review realism. Pass bar: no OCR regression, decimal stddev under one cell, and clear realism lift on the 8-merchant matrix.

**Disagreements**
`thermal-sans-mono` is tempting but GPL-2 is the wrong default for a repo that may ship demo assets. Faker/uszipcode/usaddress are over-engineered here; real corpus templates beat fake generators. Augraphy before grid typography is wasted effort. ReceiptLine/ESC-POS runtimes are unnecessary; copy the column algorithm. Random QR/barcode drawings are not “synthetic but plausible”; they are visibly fake.
tokens used
106,771
Plan: kill per-token rendering first; grid typography is the blocker, and texture/graphics only matter after that.

**1. Typography**
D1 Font: adopt VileR Ultimate Oldschool PC Font Pack `Bm437 IBM VGA 8x16` as the bundled default. It matches Epson Font A’s 8x16/0.5-ish grid better than VT323, avoids GPL font redistribution risk from `thermal-sans-mono`, and is acceptable for demo/training with attribution.

D2 Code: add `rendering/receipt_grid.py` with `build_grid_spec`, `group_words_into_grid_lines`, `draw_grid_line`, `draw_token_chars`. Change [receipt_renderer.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/rendering/receipt_renderer.py:77) `render_receipt` to group by line, pick one font size per line, set `draw.fontmode = "1"`, and place each glyph at `grid_left + col * cell_w` with `anchor="ls"`. Keep `_fit_font`/`_fit_condense` only for an explicit legacy fallback. Change `_draw_text` into the grid glyph drawer. Change `_load_font` to prefer the vendored Bm437 font. Extend [font_profile.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/rendering/font_profile.py:119) `MerchantFontProfile.to_geometry_params` with `cell_w_px`, `cell_h_px`, `estimated_columns`. Change [render_synthetic_receipts.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/scripts/render_synthetic_receipts.py:548) `_render_cached_hybrid` to enable grid mode and stop using `min_font_px/max_font_px` as the realism control.

D3 Dependencies: no pip dependency beyond Pillow. Add vendored TTF plus `NOTICE`/attribution. Offline risk is font availability; fail closed to existing system monospace only for tests.

D4 Order: first. Nothing else should be judged before this lands.

**2. Layout**
D1 Library: adopt `python-escpos` `software_columns` algorithm, but vendor our own 40-line MIT-attributed implementation. Do not add `python-escpos` or ReceiptLine at runtime.

D2 Code: extend `rendering/receipt_grid.py` with `GridCell`, `GridLine`, `layout_cells`, `wrap_cell`, `token_spans_to_bboxes`. Change [merchant_synthesis.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/receipt_agent/receipt_agent/agents/label_evaluator/merchant_synthesis.py:6453) `_line_step` and `_label_x_p50` to prefer grid metadata when present. Change `_template_fill_geometry`, `_build_template_filled_row`, `_build_line_item_line`, `_build_line`, `_right_align_money_box` to emit desc/price/tax-flag cells instead of freehand token rectangles. Change `render_receipt` to render a full grid line when `line["grid"]` exists, else infer grid from word boxes.

D3 Dependencies: stdlib `textwrap` only. Risk: wrapped item rows differ by merchant; make wrap policy per merchant profile.

D4 Order: second, immediately after typography. Can parallelize tests/metrics with content work once the grid API is stable.

**3. Content**
D1 Library: adopt `phonenumbers` only. Do not add Faker, faker-commerce, uszipcode, or usaddress for the demo path; use real corpus text plus static merchant profiles.

D2 Code: add `synthesis_content_profile.py` and `synthesis_receipt_model.py` for merchant grammar, tax letters, item-count semantics, and totals validation. Change `generate_merchant_synthesis_candidates` to attach a content profile and reject invalid candidates before return. Change `_compose_online_catalog_receipt`, `_write_composed_totals`, `_apply_non_taxable_delta`, `_apply_taxable_delta`, `_reconcile_item_count` to use one pure reconciliation function with hard assertions. Keep `synthesis_text_clean.clean_token_text` as a cleanup pass, not a generator.

D3 Dependencies: `phonenumbers`. Runtime risk is tiny. Static ZIP/address tables are safer than fake-data libraries for this use case.

D4 Order: third. Can run in parallel with graphics after item #2 defines row/cell grammar.

**4. Graphics**
D1 Library: adopt `treepoem` as the one graphics generator. It handles Code128, UPC-A, I2of5, and QR through BWIPP; standards-correct HRI beats the current fake random bars.

D2 Code: add `rendering/receipt_graphics.py` with `render_barcode_tile`, `render_qr_tile`, `graphics_profile_for_merchant`. Replace [render_synthetic_receipts.py](/Users/tnorlund/Portfolio_content/scripts/render_synthetic_receipts.py:674) `_draw_qr` and `_draw_barcode`; change `_overlay_qr_and_barcode` to paste generated tiles into real blank bands; keep `_overlay_cached_logo` but route logos through the same final degradation pass. Add merchant placement hints from `merchant_synthesis` metadata where available.

D3 Dependencies: `treepoem` pip plus system Ghostscript. Offline/CI risk is `gs` missing; detect once at startup and skip graphics with an explicit warning rather than silently drawing fake bars.

D4 Order: fourth. Can prototype independently on cached renders after typography lands.
